SELECT "o"."Id", "o"."OrderDate", "o"."TotalPrice", "o"."Status", "u"."Username", "u"."Id", "s"."ProductName", "s"."Quantity", "s"."Price", "s"."Id", "s"."Id0"
FROM "Orders" AS "o"
INNER JOIN "Users" AS "u" ON "o"."UserId" = "u"."Id"
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT "p"."Name" AS "ProductName", "o0"."Quantity", "o0"."Price", "o0"."Id", "p"."Id" AS "Id0", "o0"."OrderId"
    FROM "OrderItems" AS "o0"
    INNER JOIN "Products" AS "p" ON "o0"."ProductId" = "p"."Id"

SELECT "o"."Id", "o"."OrderDate", "o"."TotalPrice", "o"."Status", "u"."Username", "u"."Id", "s"."ProductName", "s"."Quantity", "s"."Price", "s"."Id", "s"."Id0"
FROM "Orders" AS "o"
INNER JOIN "Users" AS "u" ON "o"."UserId" = "u"."Id"
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT "p"."Name" AS "ProductName", "o0"."Quantity", "o0"."Price", "o0"."Id", "p"."Id" AS "Id0", "o0"."OrderId"
    FROM "OrderItems" AS "o0"
    INNER JOIN "Products" AS "p" ON "o0"."ProductId" = "p"."Id"
) AS "s" ON "o"."Id" = "s"."OrderId"
